================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_F-150/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_F-150/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_F-150/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_F-150/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_F-150/Config/Modules/Reverselights.lua ---

--[[
    Reverselights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local reverselights = body.Reverselights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, reverselights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_F-150/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command F-150 → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
			return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
				
				local Spotlight = spotlight;
				local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
				local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
				
				local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
				
				if subevent == 'Enable' then
				
					Light.Enabled = event;
					Beam.Enabled = event;
					spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
					
				elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
					if angle == 'Left' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Right' then
						Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
					elseif angle == 'Halt' then
						Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;

--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_Tahoe/Config/ELSPatterns/Pattern1.lua ---

--[[
    Pattern1 (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command Tahoe → Config → ELSPatterns
    Parent: ELSPatterns
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2);
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1);
	local T1 = elsModule(ELSModel.T1);
	local T2 = elsModule(ELSModel.T2);
	local O1 = elsModule(ELSModel.O1);
	local O2 = elsModule(ELSModel.O2);
	local V2 = elsModule(ELSModel.V2);
	local V1 = elsModule(ELSModel.V1);
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					T1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					T2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0);
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					B1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					B2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0.09);
					B1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					B2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0.09);
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					O1(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					O2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0);
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					V2(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.09);
					V1(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					V2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0.09);
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()			
				while true do
					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));					
					wait(0.09)	
					F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F4(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));					
					wait(0.09)	
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		F2(1);
		F1(1);
		F3(1);
		F4(1);
		B2(1);
		B1(1);
		T1(1);
		T2(1);
		O1(1);
		O2(1);
		V1(1);
		V2(1);
	end
end

					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					F2(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F3(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F4(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));					
					wait(0.12)						

					F1(1);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.09)						

					F1(0);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(0);					
					wait(0.12)					

					F1(1);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.09)						

					F1(1);	
					F2(0);	
					F3(0);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.12)						

					F1(1);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.09)						

					F1(1);	
					F2(0);	
					F3(0);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.12)						

					F1(1);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.09)							


					F1(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));
					F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(1, Color3.fromRGB(248, 248, 248));					
					wait(0.12)						

					F1(1);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.09)						

					F1(1);	
					F2(0);	
					F3(0);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.12)					

					F1(1);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.09)						

					F1(0);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(0);					
					wait(0.12)						

					F1(1);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.09)						

					F1(0);	
					F2(1);

					F4(0);					
					wait(0.12)					

					F1(1);	
					F2(1);	
					F3(1);	
					F4(1);					
					wait(0.09)						

				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		F2(1);
		F1(1);
		F3(1);
		F4(1);
		B2(1);
		B1(1);
		T1(1);
		T2(1);
		O1(1);
		O2(1);
		V1(1);
		V2(1);
	end
end



================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Brakelights.lua ---

--[[
    Brakelights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, headlightsState, enabled)
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	elseif not headlightsState then
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_Tahoe/Config/Modules/ElsPart.lua ---

--[[
    ElsPart (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function(part)
	return function(transparency, colour)
		if not part:GetAttribute('TD') then
			part.Transparency = (transparency)
			if colour then
				if typeof(colour) == "BrickColor" then
					part.BrickColor = colour;
				elseif typeof(colour) == "Color3" then
					part.Color = colour;
				end;
			end;
			if part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight') then
				local a = part:FindFirstChildOfClass('SpotLight');
				a.Enabled = (transparency == 0 and true or false)
				if colour then
					a.Color = (typeof(colour) == 'Color3' and colour or colour.Color)
				end
			end;
		end;
		
	end;
end

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Headlights.lua ---

--[[
    Headlights (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, enabled)
	local headlights = body.Headlights.Union;
	local brakelights = body.Brakelights;

	if enabled then
		headlights.Material = neonMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = true;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = true;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = neonMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = true;
		end;
	else
		headlights.Material = smoothMaterial;
		headlights.Light.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam.Enabled = false;
		headlights.LightBeam2.Enabled = false;
		for i, v in next, brakelights:GetChildren() do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;


================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Indicators.lua ---

--[[
    Indicators (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
local neonMaterial = Enum.Material.Neon;
local smoothMaterial = Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;

return function(body, side, enabled, wait)
	local indicators = body[(side == -1) and 'LeftIndicators' or 'RightIndicators']:GetChildren();

	if enabled then
		while true do
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = neonMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = true;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
			for i, v in next, indicators do
				v.Material = smoothMaterial;
				v.Light.Enabled = false;
			end;
			wait(0.5);
		end;
	else
		for i, v in next, indicators do
			v.Material = smoothMaterial;
			v.Light.Enabled = false;
		end;
	end;
end;

================================================================================
--- SCRIPT PATH: ReplicatedStorage/Cars/Correctional_Service_Canada/CSC_Command_Tahoe/Config/Modules/Spotlight.lua ---

--[[
    Spotlight (ModuleScript)
    Path: ReplicatedStorage → Cars → Correctional Service Canada → CSC Command Tahoe → Config → Modules
    Parent: Modules
    Exported: 2026-04-17 17:07:42
]]
return function (spotlight, event, subevent, angle)
	
	local Spotlight = spotlight;
	local Beam = spotlight.Center.Casing.LightBeam;
	local Light = spotlight.Center.Casing.Light;
	
	local Hinge = Spotlight.Center.Pivot.HingeConstraint;
	
	if subevent == 'Enable' then
	
		Light.Enabled = event;
		Beam.Enabled = event;
		spotlight.Center.LED1.Material = (event == true and Enum.Material.Neon) or Enum.Material.SmoothPlastic;
		
	elseif subevent == 'Rotate' then
		if angle == 'Left' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = 90;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Right' then
			Hinge.TargetAngle = -80;
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 3;
		elseif angle == 'Halt' then
			Hinge.AngularSpeed = 0;
		end;
	end;
end;

					K2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					V1(1, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					V2(1, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0.09);
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		B5(1)
		B6(1)
		B7(1)
		B8(1)
		LS1(1)
		LS2(1)
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		RS1(1)
		RS2(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)
		F7(1)
		F8(1)
		K1(1)
		K2(1)
		V1(1)
		V2(1)
	end
end

local elsModule = require(script.Parent.Parent.Modules.ElsPart);
return function(ELSModel, enabled, wait)
	local B5 = elsModule(ELSModel.B5);
	local B6 = elsModule(ELSModel.B6);
	local B7 = elsModule(ELSModel.B7);
	local B8 = elsModule(ELSModel.B8);
	local LS1 = elsModule(ELSModel.LS1);
	local LS2 = elsModule(ELSModel.LS2);
	local F1 = elsModule(ELSModel.F1);
	local F2 = elsModule(ELSModel.F2);
	local F3 = elsModule(ELSModel.F3);
	local F4 = elsModule(ELSModel.F4);
	local B1 = elsModule(ELSModel.B1);
	local B2 = elsModule(ELSModel.B2);
	local B3 = elsModule(ELSModel.B3);
	local B4 = elsModule(ELSModel.B4);
	local RS1 = elsModule(ELSModel.RS1);
	local RS2 = elsModule(ELSModel.RS2);
	local F5 = elsModule(ELSModel.F5);
	local F6 = elsModule(ELSModel.F6);
	local F7 = elsModule(ELSModel.F7);
	local F8 = elsModule(ELSModel.F8);
	local K1 = elsModule(ELSModel.K1);
	local K2 = elsModule(ELSModel.K2);
	local V1 = elsModule(ELSModel.V1);
	local V2 = elsModule(ELSModel.V2);
	if enabled then
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					B5(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					B6(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					B7(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					B8(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 101, 101));
					LS1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					LS2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F3(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					F4(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					B1(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					B2(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					B3(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					B4(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					RS1(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					RS2(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					F5(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					F6(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					F7(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					F8(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0);
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					K1(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					K2(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					wait(0);
				end
			end)
		end)
		task.spawn(function()
			pcall(function()
				while true do
					V1(0, Color3.fromRGB(255, 89, 89));
					V2(0, Color3.fromRGB(74, 116, 255));
					wait(0);
				end
			end)
		end)
	else
		B5(1)
		B6(1)
		B7(1)
		B8(1)
		LS1(1)
		LS2(1)
		F1(1)
		F2(1)
		F3(1)
		F4(1)
		B1(1)
		B2(1)
		B3(1)
		B4(1)
		RS1(1)
		RS2(1)
		F5(1)
		F6(1)
		F7(1)
		F8(1)
		K1(1)
		K2(1)
		V1(1)
		V2(1)
	end
end
